2026-03-26 13:38:09.945 INFO  [API_PROCESSING] [348a8591-246d-41ab-9577-bd91ff9e40f7] [anonymous] [EmpVacationQueryProcessor_Subclass] [or.so.ea.tm.se.EmpVacationQueryService] (executor-thread-1) [???u???O?M??] ??R?? - effectiveDate: 'null', deptCode: null, empNo: 'null', empName: 'null'
[Hibernate] 
    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        ) 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        )   
        AND YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE) = ? 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        )   
        AND e.ORG_ID = ? 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        )   
        AND e.EMP_ACCOUNT LIKE ? 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        )   
        AND e.EMP_NAME LIKE ? 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

2026-03-26 13:38:10.959 INFO  [API_PROCESSING] [af1067b5-9913-414b-ab3e-1f0d1774243f] [anonymous] [EmpVacationQueryProcessor_Subclass] [or.so.ea.tm.se.EmpVacationQueryService] (executor-thread-2) [???u???O?M??] ??R?? - effectiveDate: 'null', deptCode: null, empNo: 'null', empName: 'null'
[Hibernate] 
    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        ) 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        ) 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT DESC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

2026-03-26 13:38:11.100 INFO  [API_PROCESSING] [3ce325f3-e8cf-445d-97e9-40f18061c8b9] [anonymous] [EmpVacationQueryProcessor_Subclass] [or.so.ea.tm.se.EmpVacationQueryService] (executor-thread-2) [???u???O?M??] ??R?? - effectiveDate: 'null', deptCode: null, empNo: 'null', empName: 'null'

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        ) 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

    SELECT
        v.EMP_VACATION_ID       AS quotaId,
        v.EMP_ID                AS empId,
        YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE)      AS year,
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT           AS empNo,
        e.EMP_NAME              AS empNameCh,
        e.EMP_NAME_EN           AS empNameEn,
        org.ORG_ID              AS deptCode,
        org.ORG_NAME            AS deptName,
        vds.VACATION_CODE       AS vacationCode,
        vs.VACATION_NAME        AS vacationName,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_CODE   AS vacationSubCode,
        vds.VACATION_SUB_NAME   AS vacationSubName,
        v.BEGIN_DATE            AS effectiveStartDate,
        v.END_DATE              AS effectiveEndDate,
        v.MAX_HOURS             AS totalHours,
        v.USED_HOURS            AS usedHours,
        v.UNUSED_HOURS          AS remainingHours,
        v.CLEAR                 AS settlementStatus,
        v.CASH_OUT_HOURS        AS cashOutHours 
    FROM
        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.PM_EMPLOYEE e     
            ON e.EMP_ID = v.EMP_ID 
    LEFT JOIN
        EAP.AU_ORGANIZATION org     
            ON org.ORG_ID = e.ORG_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        (
            e.LEAVE_DATE IS NULL 
            OR e.LEAVE_DATE >= GETDATE()
        )   
        AND YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE) = ?   
        AND e.EMP_ACCOUNT LIKE ? 
    ORDER BY
        e.EMP_ACCOUNT ASC,
        vds.VACATION_CODE ASC

        EAP.TM_EMP_VACATION v 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_DETAIL_SETTING vds     
            ON vds.VACATION_SUB_ID = v.VACATION_SUB_ID 
    INNER JOIN
        EAP.TM_VACATION_SETTING vs     
            ON vs.VACATION_CODE = vds.VACATION_CODE 
    WHERE
        v.EMP_ID = ?   
        AND YEAR(v.BEGIN_DATE) = ? 
    ORDER BY
        v.VACATION_SUB_ID
